           <dd>&#x2022; element, primitive matter (= <em>mah&#x0101;-bh&#x016b;ta</em> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a>) <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#MBh">MBh.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Hariv">Hariv.</a> &amp;c.            <dd>&#x2022; to which is added <em>brahma</em> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Y&#x0101;j&#x00f1;">Y&#x0101;j&#x00f1;.</a> iii, 145 </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or <em>vij&#x00f1;&#x0101;na</em> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Buddh">Buddh.</a>) </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; a constituent element or essential ingredient of the body (distinct from the 5 mentioned above and conceived either as 3 humours [called also <em>do&#x1e63;a</em>] phlegm, wind and bile <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#BhP">BhP.</a> [cf. <em>pur&#x012b;&#x1e63;a</em>, <em>m&#x0101;&#x1e43;sa</em>, <em>manas</em>, Ch&#x0101;ndUp. vi, 5, 1] </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or as the 5 organs of sense, <em>indriy&#x0101;&#x1e47;i</em> .[<a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#s">s.</a>v. and <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#MBh">MBh.</a> xii, 6842, where <em>&#x015b;rotra</em>, <em>ghr&#x0101;&#x1e47;a</em>, <em>&#x0101;sya</em>, <em>h&#x1e5b;daya</em> and <em>ko&#x1e63;&#x1e6d;ha</em> are mentioned as the 5 dh&#x0101;tu of the human body born from the either] and the 5 properties of the elements perceived by them, <em>gandha</em>, <em>rasa</em>, <em>r&#x016b;pa</em>, <em>spar&#x015b;a</em> and <em>&#x015b;abda</em> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a> </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or the 7 fluids or secretions, chyle, blood, flesh, fat, bone, marrow, semen <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Su&#x015b;r">Su&#x015b;r.</a> [<a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a> <em>ras&#x00e2;di</em> or <em>rasa-rakt&#x00e2;di</em>, of which sometimes 10 are given, the above 7 and hair, skin, sinews <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#BhP">BhP.</a>]) </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; primary element of the earth, i.e. metal, mineral, are (esp. a mineral of a red colour) <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Mn">Mn.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#MBh">MBh.</a> &amp;c. element of words, i.e. grammatical or verbal &#x221a;or stem <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Nir">Nir.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Pr&#x0101;t">Pr&#x0101;t.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#MBh">MBh.</a> &amp;c. (with the southern Buddhists <em>dh&#x0101;tu</em> means either the 6 elements <em>see above</em> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Dharmas">Dharmas.</a> xxv </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or the 18 elementary spheres [<em>dh&#x0101;tu-loka</em>] <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#ib">ib.</a> lviii </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or the ashes of the body, relics <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a> [cf. <em>-garbha</em>])</dd>
